 ) bhartiya rigerv bank ne vibhinn card len-dein main suraksha ko or majboot banane ke lihaaj se nai 'token' vyavastha apnaane ke vaaste dishanirdesh jari kiye, inamen debit or credit card se len-dein bhi shaamil hai
 The purpose of this token system is to strengthen the security of the payment system
 iskaa taatpary card ke vaastavik byore ko ek vishisht vaikalpik code token se badalanaa he, yah code apane aap main ek vishisht vyavastha hogi
 The point-of-sale (POS) terminals, Quick Response (QR) codes, are used instead of the actual card details for payment, this token is used for transactions in a card-free manner
 kendriya bank ne kaha ki token card se len-dein kii suvidha philhal mobile phone or tablet ke jariye uplabdh hogi, isse praapt anubhav ke aadhaar par baad main iskaa vistaar anya upkarnon tak kiya jayega
 The Reserve Bank's release stated that the tokenization of cards and removal from the token system will be done only by the authorized card network, in which recovery of the original primary account number (PAN) will also be done from the authorized card network
 graahak ko is seva ko lene ke liye koi shulk nahin dena hoga
